name:R‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçb‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçg‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äç0‚Äç4‚Äç2‚Äç1
info:Deluxe Family Parent-child Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Friends
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:I often watch the live broadcast of An Ying, vice president of Blue Ocean Group, on a certain platform. The corporate culture of the hotel is worthy of recognition!
This trip to Tai'an Blue Ocean, the first thing worth praising is that the overall service is very good. The hotel is basically a trip to Mount Tai during the holidays. The lobby staff is warm and thoughtful, listens carefully, responds to requests, has a friendly attitude, and can meet the needs of guests in a timely manner. There is a live broadcast TV of Mount Tai in the lobby on the first floor, which is very considerate. The hotel is conveniently located, and it takes more than ten minutes to take a taxi from the Hongmen Mountain Entrance, and less than ten minutes to the Dai Temple. There is a shopping mall across the road, which is convenient for parking and travel.
Talking about the shortcomings, I think the overall hardware facilities of Tai'an Yuhua are not as good as Weihai Yuhua. The room facilities are a bit aging, especially the furniture and decoration in the room. The wallpaper is worn and damaged, and the carpet is a bit faded, giving people a sense of oldness. In addition, the maintenance of some facilities also needs to be strengthened, such as the toilet glass is flowery, some mirror lights are not bright, the kettle has obvious water stains, and the toilet has peculiar smell.
The breakfast is not satisfactory. As a quasi-five-star hotel, the buffet breakfast is poor in both process management and food supply. First, there is a lack of management staff to inquire and guide tourists to the buffet restaurant, which feels a bit like a large canteen; second, there are many dishes but not refined, Western baked desserts are few in variety and taste poor, only bacon and grilled sausages are not available, and the variety of jams and cold salad dressings is limited; the most important thing is the third point of sanitation management and plating. The coffee machine and beverage machine are all stained with water on the floor, the fried eggs are in an unsightly pile, the cereal and milk area are scattered everywhere, and the plastic tea cups are old and dirty. The service staff only cleaned the table, and the lack of dishes and dishes was not discovered and replenished in time. The overall mental outlook of the breakfast depar**ent service staff is average.
In short, Tai'an Blue Sea Yuhua Hotel performed well overall, and the service is worthy of recognition. I hope Tai'an Yuhua can continue to work hard to make up for the shortcomings and enhance the new image of Taishan tourism!

msg:This hotel is probably the best hotel in Tai'an. I booked a family room, which is very spacious and has a very large bathroom. The bathtub, shower, and toilet are all in separate areas, and the glass partition is frosted, which is convenient for the whole family to use. It's very considerate. The hotel is in a good location, not far from the red gate at the entrance of Mount Tai, and it only takes 10 yuan to get there by taxi. The breakfast is very rich, and you can climb Mount Tai after eating.
But the taxis in Tai'an feel very bad. When you come out of the train station, the short-distance ones refuse to take you. You need to bend down and communicate with the driver where to go when you take a taxi, like an uncle. It's hard to find a taxi that doesn't refuse to take you, but it's annoying when you get on the car. The car is equipped with a stainless steel cage to protect the driver, and the co-pilot's seat is very narrow, like being locked in a cage. This is something that only existed in the 1990s. It gives me the feeling that there are still taxi robbers in Tai'an, this place is not safe! I don't know if the leaders of Tai'an and Shandong think so.
